MORA (SUN) 09/13/1981 Palacio de los Deportes, Iztacalco, Distrito Federal [Box Y Lucha 1504, Halcon Monthly 4, http://wrestlingclassics.com/.ubb/ultimatebb.php?ubb=get_topic;f=10;t=005181 Matt Farmer]Attendance: 20000
1) Kobayashi, Saito vs Kurisu, Scorpió
## Halcon lists Saito moved up a match, so maybe Gran Hamada ende dup here.
2) Osamu Kido, Saito DQ Cesar Valentino, Coloso Colosetti
3) Blue Demon, Enrique Vera, Rayo de Jalisco DQ Babe Face, Choi Sun, Perro Aguayo
4) el Signo, Negro Navarro, Texano b Fishman, Huracán Ramírez, Mano Negra
5) Canek  (c) b Pat Patterson [UWA Heavy]
6) Ray Mendoza b Apeman
## A five round fight. Unclear the length of each round. Apeman clearly wins the first two rounds and is on the way to winning three when Mendoza catches him in an armbar; the bell saves him. Mendoza suplexes and submits Apeman in round 4 to win. Apeman (also listed as Ape Man) is Rick McIntosh, billed as an undefeated karate fighter. This appears to be a take on Antonio Inoki's different style fights in NJPW.

** EMLL 48th Aniversario *
1) Yanco DRAW Bufalo Salvaje
2) Fuerza Guerrera  (c) DCOR Negro Casas [DF LIGHT]
## first defense, and a rematch of a career making MOTYC match for both earlier in the tournament on 09/01. Guerrera won the tournament final last week. Casas won fall 1 with a casita (referred to as a La Magistral for the first time I can recall) in eight minutes, Fuerza took fall in 2 minutes, third ended after ten minutes when Negro Casas did a reverse tope to the floor (!) and knocked them both out. MOTYC again,more than 2000 pesos thrown in the ring as tribute.
3) El Faraón, Satánico DQ Ringo Mendoza, Tony Salazar
## DQ on Salazar for returning after being eliminated

## Vengador is Arturo Diaz Rodriguez from Gudalajra, 11 years a wrestler. Espectro Jr. challenged Supremo for the MEX WELTER

## straight falls

## Mendoza took 2/3, his third win in under a month (Satanico and Divino Roy)
